<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>мат</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">matte</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mátovyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ма́товее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ма́товей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>matte, dull, lustreless
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поверхность.html>пове́рхность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátovaja</b> povérxnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>dead</b> surface, <b>matte</b> surface</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:золото.html>зо́лото</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátovoje</b> zóloto</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>matte</b> gold</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátovaja</b> kóža</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>matte</b> leather</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>opaque, frosted
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátovoje</b> stekló</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>frosted</b> glass</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***матрас.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:матрас.html>матра́с</a> (10484)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матрас.html>матра́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">matrás</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матрас.html>матра́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матрас.html>матра́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матрас.html>матра́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mattress <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a pad on which a person can recline and sleep</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:жена.html>жена́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:матрос.html>матро́са</a>, женщина-матрос</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:матроска.html>матро́ску</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:матроска.html>матро́сок</a></i>).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-матрос-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-к</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***мать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>мать</a> (219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*méh₂tēr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>мать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">matʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́тери</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́тери</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>матере́й</a></b>)
</p>

***мах.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>мах</a> (7805)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>мах</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">max</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>ма́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>ма́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>ма́хов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>single rapid movement in the air, swing, wave, flap, stroke</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rapid forward, backward or sideways movement of the foot or hand</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mechanics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> single revolution, swing, stroke</li>
<li>step <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of an animal, usually a horse, when running</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***махавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:махавший.html>маха́вший</a> (2480)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махавший.html>маха́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxávšij</span>)
</p>

***махать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a> (2480)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*māxàti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помахать.html>помаха́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wave, to flap, to fling, to brandish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">кто́-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>ма́шет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руко́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Któ-to <b>mášet</b> tebé rukój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Someone is <b>waving</b> a hand at you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>ма<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ха́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a>.
<a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 1a: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ешь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ем</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ете</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ют</a></i>.

***махнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a> (1650)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wave, to flap, to fling, to brandish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помнить.html>по́мнишь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руко́й</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pómnišʹ, kak ty <b>maxnúl</b> mne čérez dorógu rukój?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you remember how you <b>waved</b> at me across the road?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руко́й</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maxnútʹ</b> rukój (na)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give up on someone / something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rush, to leap, to jump
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забор.html>забо́р</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>maxnúl</b> čérez zabór.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>leapt</b> over the fence.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go (off), to travel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махнём</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыбалка.html>рыба́лку</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Daváj <b>maxnjóm</b> na rybálku!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Let's go fishing!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гля́дя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maxnútʹ</b> ne gljádja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">swap without looking (i.e. recklessly)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>мах</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>

Зализняка — 3b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a>.

***махорка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́рка</a> (10181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Modification of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*амерфо́ртский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*amerfórtskij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amersfoort" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Amersfoort">Amersfoort</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the Dutch city of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amersfoort" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Amersfoort">Amersfoort</a>, known for its tobacco industries.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A coarse, strong type of tobacco, makhorka (<i>Nicotiana rustica</i>)</li></ol>

<p><b>ма<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:хор.html>хо́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> makhorka <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a strong type of tobacco</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мохра́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">moxrá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мох.html>мох</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mox</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; respelled according to pronunciation.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махра.html>махра́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxrá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махра.html>махры́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махровый.html>махро́вый</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нка</a> (3549)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mašína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mašínka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mašína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: small car, machine or mechanism</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mašína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>miniature or toy car</li>
<li>small device for accomplishing work (e.g. typewriter, washing machine, clipper, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швейный.html>шве́йная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">švéjnaja mašínka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sewing machine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> typewriter</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ма<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:шина.html>ши́н</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-машин-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-к</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> machine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:машинный.html>маши́нные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>ча́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mašínnyje</b> části</i> ― <span class="e-translation">machinery/engine parts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:машинный.html>маши́нное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mašínnoje</b> máslo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">machine/engine oil</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:машинный.html>маши́нное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отделение.html>отделе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mašínnoje</b> otdelénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">engine room</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделанный.html>сде́ланный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:машинный.html>маши́нным</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:способ.html>спо́собом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sdélannyj <b>mašínnym</b> spósobom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">machine-made</span></div></dd>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> computer

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:машинный.html>маши́нное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:моделирование.html>модели́рование</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:проектирование.html>проекти́рование</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mašínnoje</b> modɛlírovanije/proektírovanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">computer-aided design</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***маяк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:маяк.html>мая́к</a> (8916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маяк.html>мая́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maják</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маяк.html>маяка́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маяк.html>мая́ка</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маяк.html>маяки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маяк.html>маяко́в</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Nautical language sometimes keeps the stress on the stem.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>lighthouse</li>
<li>beacon</li>
<li>Used as the call sign for some <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soyuz" class="extiw" title="w:Soyuz">Soyuz</a> missions: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soyuz_T-3" class="extiw" title="w:Soyuz T-3">Soyuz T-3</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soyuz_T-10" class="extiw" title="w:Soyuz T-10">Soyuz T-10</a> amp; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soyuz_T-15" class="extiw" title="w:Soyuz T-15">Soyuz T-15</a>.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:маять.html>ма́янный</a> (21913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
